< text>
I came in for a quick visit and met so many REALLY genuine people here.  I'm working on learning basic crossfit and how to do the rope climb. The normal members that come to this gym are SUCH nice people.  They saw me struggling and stopped to give me tips and to help me learn. I was scaling the rope (poorly, but could climb it) by the time I walked out of the facility 40 minutes later.  Clean, lots of state of the art, top end equipment, spacious, and a great / friendly staff.  Would highly recommend dropping in and checking them out.  WELL worth the stop.  Thank you guys so much!</text>

< review>
I have been going to Crossfit Tustin for almost three years now, and I love everything about it. The people are all top notch, the programming is on point, and it's just a fun place to be. The space is large, and well kept, and management has done a good job of adding value to the membership. Coach consultations, body scanning, personal training, meal plans, skills courses, and recovery options are all available on site, which keeps members engaged for more than just the class workouts. Having traveled to many different boxes around the world, I can safely say that Tustin sets the bar across the board.< /review>

< text>
Great place to get in shape. The coaches are very knowledgeable, friendly and really take the time to breakdown the technical aspects of the exercises. The workouts are very well rounded with a good balance of cardio, Olympic weight lifting, core and accessory work. Crossfit Tustin also stands out with the implementation of ROM WODs. A yogaesque stretching session -usually done after Thursday workouts- that really helps alleviate lactic acid build up from previous work outs. My favorite aspect of the Crossfit Tustin's business model is the sense of community they create. Joel and his team do a great job at encouraging that sense of community by organising lots of fun in-house events and also by supporting and promoting lots of community events. This is most evident in the member's support of each other during tough work outs. All in all Crossfit Tustin's well balanced workout regiments and friendly members makes it fun to get in shape on your way to becoming an elite athlete. Thank you Joel and team for all you do!<//text>

< Text>
Hands down THE best Crossfit gym in OC!! I tried 4 different gyms in the area and this one is by far the best. I went to many different crossfit boxes whenever I traveled and crossfit Tustin is by far the best!!

Good mix of Male/ Female coaches, programming is great and challenging, lots of classes at different time of the day, also open gym hours.

Mix of super fit competitive crossfit athletes and ‚Äúnormal‚Äù people LOL

Even if everyone is on his own fitness journey (losing or gaining weight, gaining muscles/ strength, working of specific weightlifting skills, competing in crossfit‚Ä¶) everyone mix well together.

Joel, the owner, is also very connected with a lot of health specialist in the area, when I first started to workout there I asked him if he could help me find a good chiropractor in the area and he recommended me one. She helped me a ton with an old neck injury I was struggling with for years. If you need help with an injury or with nutrition, they have coaches or qualified people they can recommend you.

There‚Äôs also a massage therapist, who is at the gym for a couple hours every Friday, very helpful if you need some advice or some body work done!

Equipment: they have a lot of EVERYTHING (Assault bikes, rowers, ski erg, peg board, tons of free weights, barbells) and it‚Äôs well maintained! They have a big bright space (lots of daylight) and high ceilings, great for rope climbs!

If you workout there regularly, BONUS you will also meet Bentley & Maverick, the gym dogs!!! They are awesome and bring even more life into the place :-)

The only downside is that it‚Äôs a bit pricey, but it‚Äôs California, everything is more expensive here and you get what you pay for! I‚Äôve been to other gyms who were charging a bit less, but the quality of the coaching/ equipment/ space was nothing compared to this place! If you want results, this is the place to go to! Thank you Joel, Adam, Jevon, Aaron, Megan, Chris‚Ä¶and all the other coaches!!</Text>

< Review>
Crossfit always sounded crazy intense to me and I was never a competitive "sports sports sports!" type of person so I was very nervous to try it out. However, Crossfit Tustin is so unbelievably welcoming and warm that you feel at home as soon as you step in the door. Everyone is friendly and genuinely excited to meet you and to work out with you. There's no pressure there to be better than anyone else - the only goal is to improve upon your own skills and to try your hardest. It's a true community that not all Crossfit boxes have and I've never felt stronger, more confident in my own abilities, or more connected to so many fantastic and inspiring people.<//Review>

< Review>
This review is written 3 months after I got coolsculpting done in 6 different areas. This was my first time doing it so I was quite hesitant but Patrick was very informative during the consultation and addressed all my concerns around the procedure in a transparent way. My biggest concern was the possibility of coolsculpting backfiring and causing paradoxical adipose hyperplasia. Patrick reassured me and told me that the chances of this happening were very small.
The procedure itself went smoothly. I had redness and swelling immediately after, which quickly resolved in a few days.
Around a month post procedure, I started feeling the results as my clothes fit more loosely. The problem areas I had the procedure on were definitely smaller. I am a petite person so it'd be very difficult for me to achieve the same results through exercise and dieting alone. I feel like coolsculpting was definitely worth it!<//Review>

Dr. Korman is very professional and his staff are extremely kind and helpful.  I feel like I can return for procedures without feeling much stress or concern. There were a few raised areas, one in the middle was particularly bumpy.  I was worried that they were keloid scars and I had heard those are difficult to correct.  When I met Dr. Korman, he took a look at the scar and informed me that what I had was actually hypertrophic scarring which is much easier to treat.  He reassured me that he could repair these areas without cutting the entire scar again.  On the day of the surgery, he was very patient and kind with me. The team made sure I was comfortable and ready for the resection.  During the procedure, Dr. Korman made sure that I had enough numbing agent so that I could not feel the cuts. He offered my steroid injections as a part of the surgical fee and explained that I had the option of using silicone bandages as well. I have always had a hard time losing the fat on my lower abdomen above my pelvis. I am generally thin, so my little pot belly seemed to be quite noticeable. Unlike the other surgeons I met with, Dr. Korman doesn't have a preference (or one incision site that he's most comfortable with). I got to decide for myself because he can perform with precision from any of the options. I left that day feeling informed, confident and excited!

When I went home, I began doing some research and found that he is not only an amazing mind and doctor; but, he's genuinely a great person who gives back to the community and is STILL an educator in his field at the HIGHEST Institutions in CA after already having his own practice for over 25 years. I love Sunday's where they have a fun DJ and free pool aswell as a bartender that sets the bar (pun intended) for excellent service and vibe!!< /review>

<pics>None<//pics><date>1534063988096< /date><text>I've been coming to this bar for about 5 years.  When I first started coming here, it was a life saver to me. I was new to California. I met many local amazing musicians.  In the past, Dave's offered live entertainment, open mic nights and karaoke. I sang with bands and was blessed to sing on a couple different albums.

I have mixed feelings now about coming here. It's extremely convenient for me but several visits to karaoke has left me with a feeling of disappointment and emptiness. I know that late in the night, the bar gets new young blood and they want to cater to them, but when I arrive at 11:00 with only a few names on the list, buy a couple, three drinks and get to sing one song around 1:00 a.m., I feel I have wasted money and time.

Tonight, I heard a couple other people complaining similar stories. Maybe Dave's doesn't need the neighborhood standbys anymore. I certainly don't see the regular faces I use to see.

That being said, the bartender is awesome and newcomers seem to enjoy themselves. "The times, they are a changing."</text><response>None</response>< name>

<name>Dustin Ingraham< /name><date>1602569388412</date><rate>5< /rate>< Text>
I had a small dent in my trunk for years, and I could not figure out where it came from. Every time I would go to my car, it would stand out like a sore thumb to me, even though other people claimed they couldn't see it. I finally had the time to get the dent removed, and after doing some online research and checking reviews, I decided to use this company.

I called them to arrange a time to fix my car. They came to me to perform the work, which was great. If I recall, they were not open during the weekends and were only open during business hours during the week, which made arranging the service a little more complex. (I work in a gated parking lot and I can't have unauthorized vehicles in the lot) so I had to make arrangements to leave my car at my house while I was at work.

The car technician that fixed my car showed flexibility and picked up the keys from the leasing office and performed the work on time during the promised time window.

I did not enjoy the payment experience, which is why I only rated 4-stars. I was called by the technician after he finished the work and he asked for my payment information (while I was still at work and did not have a chance to inspect the work done prior to paying--remember, the vehicle was left at my house and I got a ride into work). The tech advised me that there will be pictures attached to the invoice I receive AFTER I pay him. It's a little backwards to see what you're paying for only after you've forked over your money.

Will I use them again? Yes, absolutely. They performed quality work at a decent price, and were punctual and had good availability. Will I still be uncomfortable coughing up money before I'm able to see the work performed, yes, who wouldn't? As long as the prices stay reasonable and they have good availability though, I'll be a loyal customer :)

Update: After I left the above review, a DentPro co-owner called me to thank me for the constructive feedback and to let me know that they thought my suggestion was helpful. They did NOT ask me to come back in and edit my review, but I am choosing to do so because I think it says a lot about a company that they monitor their Google reviews and took the time to look up my contact information in their internal system and call me for no reason other than to thank me for taking the time to leave a review and for pointing out a possible area of improvement. A lot of companies these days would get defensive when possible areas of improvement are identified, but they demonstrated a willingness to improve and open-mindedness that is difficult to find in a business these days. Because of the improvements being made to the pre-payment photo review process I am adding that one star back.<//Text>

<Rating>5< /Rating>< review>
It was a pleasure working with Steve! Funny story, I actually chose him randomly from the AP Mortgage website, looked at everyone's pictures and thought, "oh, he looks like a nice guy." AP Mortgage was the preferred lender for the property I purchased and unlike other lender websites, I didn't see a way to just apply for a loan on their website. There was just a form to fill in your information to have someone contact you to give you a quote. Well, I waited a day and no one had contacted me other than an email saying someone will reach out, so me being impatient, clicked around the website and found out I can send in an application after selecting a loan officer and visiting their page!

Anyway, Steve was great! He has experience working in this field for quite some time, so he was watching the market to get me a good rate. If anything important comes up that needs to be done right away, he always calls. Everything was a breeze, no huge hiccups. He takes the time to explain things in ways I can understand, since this is my 1st home, I didn't know much of the process at all.

I went into the process with certain expectations and knowing I would need to provide alot of documentation, so I think I already had most of what was normally required. Due to my personal circumstances, Steve suggested I provide more work history to show consistency and a letter with explanation of gaps. I thought it was a great idea to be extra thorough to submit all of it in one big package! I have read other's experiences where they feel annoyed that they have to keep submitting more because the underwriter keeps requesting additional information and I did not feel any frustrations regarding that at all.

I would definitely work with Steve again if given the chance and refer him to my friends and family :)<//review>
